   - ë¼ìš°í„° ë“±ë¡ êµ¬ì¡°ë§Œ ì¤€ë¹„ (ì‹¤ì œ ë¼ìš°í„°ëŠ” Phase 6ì—ì„œ êµ¬í˜„)

### ê·œì¹™ ì¤€ìˆ˜ ì‚¬í•­

- AGENTS.md: Phase 1 ì™„ë£Œ ì‘ì—…
- backend-api-design.mdc: FastAPI ì•± ì´ˆê¸°í™” íŒ¨í„´ ì¤€ìˆ˜

### ì˜ˆìƒ ê²°ê³¼

ì´ ê³„íšìœ¼ë¡œ ì§„í–‰í• ê¹Œìš”?

# backend/main.py
- FastAPI ì•± ì¸ìŠ¤í„´ìŠ¤
- CORS ë¯¸ë“¤ì›¨ì–´
- ì˜ˆì™¸ í•¸ë“¤ëŸ¬
- Health check ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸
- ë¼ìš°í„° ë“±ë¡ (ì£¼ì„ ì²˜ë¦¬, Phase 6ì—ì„œ êµ¬í˜„)

**Cursor**

```python
"""
FastAPI ì• í”Œë¦¬ì¼€ì´ì…˜ ì§„ì…ì 

ì´ ëª¨ë“ˆì€ FastAPI ì•±ì„ ì´ˆê¸°í™”í•˜ê³ , CORS ì„¤ì •, ë¼ìš°í„° ë“±ë¡, ì˜ˆì™¸ ì²˜ë¦¬ë¥¼ êµ¬ì„±í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
"""

from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException, Request
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from typing import Dict, Any

# FastAPI ì•± ì¸ìŠ¤í„´ìŠ¤ ìƒì„±
app = FastAPI(
    title="Longtext Analysis API",
    description="Cursor IDE ì„¸ì…˜ ëŒ€í™” ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì¼ì„ íŒŒì‹±í•˜ì—¬ Timeline, Issue Cards, ì½”ë“œ ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí«ì„ ìƒì„±í•˜ëŠ” API",
    version="0.1.0",
    docs_url="/docs",
    redoc_url="/redoc",
)

# CORS ì„¤ì •
# ê°œë°œ í™˜ê²½: Next.js í”„ë¡ íŠ¸ì—”ë“œ (localhost:3000) í—ˆìš©
# í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ í™˜ê²½ì—ì„œëŠ” í™˜ê²½ ë³€ìˆ˜ë¡œ ê´€ë¦¬ ê¶Œì¥
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=[
        "http://localhost:3000",  # Next.js ê°œë°œ ì„œë²„
        "http://127.0.0.1:3000",
    ],
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)


# ì˜ˆì™¸ ì²˜ë¦¬ í•¸ë“¤ëŸ¬
@app.exception_handler(HTTPException)
async def http_exception_handler(request: Request, exc: HTTPException) -> JSONResponse:
    """HTTP ì˜ˆì™¸ ì²˜ë¦¬"""
    return JSONResponse(
        status_code=exc.status_code,
        content={"detail": exc.detail},
    )


@app.exception_handler(Exception)
async def general_exception_handler(request: Request, exc: Exception) -> JSONResponse:
    """ì¼ë°˜ ì˜ˆì™¸ ì²˜ë¦¬"""
    return JSONResponse(
        status_code=500,
        content={"detail": f"Internal server error: {str(exc)}"},
    )


# Health Check ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸
# E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ì—ì„œ ì„œë²„ ìƒíƒœ í™•ì¸ìš©
@app.get("/health")
async def health_check() -> Dict[str, str]:
    """
    ì„œë²„ ìƒíƒœ í™•ì¸ ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸
    
    Returns:
        {"status": "ok"}
    """
    return {"status": "ok"}

# Phase 6ì—ì„œ ì‹¤ì œ ë¼ìš°í„° êµ¬í˜„ ì˜ˆì •
# í˜„ì¬ëŠ” êµ¬ì¡°ë§Œ ì¤€ë¹„

# TODO: Phase 6ì—ì„œ êµ¬í˜„ ì˜ˆì •
# from backend.api.routes import parse, timeline, issues, snippets, export

## ë°ì´í„° ëª¨ë¸

### SessionMeta
```python
class SessionMeta(BaseModel):
    session_id: str
    exported_at: Optional[str]
    cursor_version: Optional[str]
    phase: Optional[int]
    subphase: Optional[int]
    source_doc: str
```

### Timeline Event
```python
class TimelineEvent(BaseModel):
    seq: int
    session_id: str
    phase: Optional[int]
    subphase: Optional[int]
    type: EventType  # status_review|plan|artifact|debug|completion|next_step|turn
    summary: str
    artifacts: List[ArtifactRef]
    snippet_refs: List[str]  # snippet_id
```

### Issue Card
```python
class IssueCard(BaseModel):
    issue_id: str
    scope: IssueScope
    title: str
    symptoms: List[str]
    root_cause: Optional[RootCause]
    evidence: List[Evidence]
    fix: List[Fix]
    validation: List[str]
    related_artifacts: List[ArtifactRef]
    snippet_refs: List[str]
```

### Snippet
```python
class Snippet(BaseModel):
    snippet_id: str
    lang: str
    code: str
    source: SnippetSource
    links: SnippetLinks
```

## ì£¼ìš” íŒŒì¼ êµ¬ì¡°

```
longtext-analysis/

## Phase 2: ë°±ì—”ë“œ íŒŒì„œ êµ¬í˜„ (ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì‹±)

**ëª©í‘œ**: Cursor export ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì¼ì„ êµ¬ì¡°í™”ëœ ë°ì´í„°ë¡œ íŒŒì‹±

### í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì •ê·œí™” (`backend/parser/normalize.py`)
- [ ] ì¤„ë°”ê¿ˆ í†µì¼ (`\r\n` â†’ `\n`, `\r` â†’ `\n`)
- [ ] BOM ì œê±° (`\ufeff`)
- [ ] ê³µë°± ì •ë¦¬ (ì½”ë“œë¸”ë¡ ì œì™¸ ì˜µì…˜)
- [ ] íŠ¸ë ˆì¼ë§ ê³µë°± ì œê±°
- [ ] ë„ˆë¬´ ê¸´ ê³µë°± ì¶•ì†Œ (3ê°œ ì´ìƒ â†’ 2ê°œ, ì½”ë“œë¸”ë¡ ì œì™¸)

### ì„¸ì…˜ ë©”íƒ€ ì¶”ì¶œ (`backend/parser/meta.py`)
- [ ] Phase ì¶”ì¶œ (ì •ê·œì‹: `(?i)\bPhase\s+(\d+)\b`)
- [ ] Subphase ì¶”ì¶œ (ì •ê·œì‹: `(?i)\bSub\s*Phase\s+(\d+)\b`)
- [ ] Exported at ì¶”ì¶œ (ì •ê·œì‹: `(?i)Exported\s+(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}[^,\n]*?(?:KST|UTC|GMT|[+\-]\d{2}:\d{2})?)`)
- [ ] Cursor version ì¶”ì¶œ (ì •ê·œì‹: `(?i)\bCursor\s+(\d+\.\d+\.\d+)\b`)
- [ ] Session ID ìƒì„± ê·œì¹™ êµ¬í˜„ (`cursor_export_{exported_at_or_fallback}`)
- [ ] ìƒë‹¨ 2000~4000 chars ë²”ìœ„ì—ì„œ best-effort ì¶”ì¶œ

### Turn ë¸”ë¡ íŒŒì‹± (`backend/parser/turns.py`)
- [ ] êµ¬ë¶„ì„ (`---`) ê¸°ì¤€ ë¶„í•  (ì •ê·œì‹: `^\s*---\s*$`)
- [ ] Speaker ì¶”ì¶œ (ì •ê·œì‹: `^\s*\*\*(User|Cursor)\*\*\s*$`)
- [ ] Body í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì¶”ì¶œ (ì½”ë“œë¸”ë¡ ì œì™¸)
- [ ] Fallback íŒŒì„œ êµ¬í˜„ (êµ¬ë¶„ì„  ì—†ì„ ë•Œ `**User**`/`**Cursor**` ë¼ë²¨ ê¸°ì¤€)
- [ ] Parse Health Check (Unknown ë¹„ìœ¨ ë†’ìœ¼ë©´ í¬ë§· ê°ì§€ ì‹¤íŒ¨ ì²˜ë¦¬)

### ì½”ë“œ ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ (`backend/parser/snippets.py`)
- [ ] ì½”ë“œíœìŠ¤ ì¶”ì¶œ (ì •ê·œì‹: ````(\w+)?\n(.*?)```)
- [ ] ì–¸ì–´ íŒë³„ (lang ëˆ„ë½ ì‹œ ë¹ˆ ë¬¸ìì—´ ì²˜ë¦¬)

## ë°ì´í„° ëª¨ë¸

### SessionMeta
```python
class SessionMeta(BaseModel):
    session_id: str
    exported_at: Optional[str]
    cursor_version: Optional[str]
    phase: Optional[int]
    subphase: Optional[int]
    source_doc: str
```

### Timeline Event
```python
class TimelineEvent(BaseModel):
    seq: int
    session_id: str
    phase: Optional[int]
    subphase: Optional[int]
    type: EventType  # status_review|plan|artifact|debug|completion|next_step|turn
    summary: str
    artifacts: List[ArtifactRef]
    snippet_refs: List[str]  # snippet_id
```

### Issue Card
```python
class IssueCard(BaseModel):
    issue_id: str
    scope: IssueScope
    title: str
    symptoms: List[str]
    root_cause: Optional[RootCause]
    evidence: List[Evidence]
    fix: List[Fix]
    validation: List[str]
    related_artifacts: List[ArtifactRef]
    snippet_refs: List[str]
```

### Snippet
```python
class Snippet(BaseModel):
    snippet_id: str
    lang: str
    code: str
    source: SnippetSource
    links: SnippetLinks
```

- Turn ë¸”ë¡ íŒŒì‹± (`backend/parser/turns.py`)
- ì½”ë“œ ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ (`backend/parser/snippets.py`)
- Artifact ì¶”ì¶œ (`backend/parser/artifacts.py`)

í”¼ë“œë°± ì£¼ì‹œë©´ Phase 2ë¡œ ì§„í–‰í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

---

**User**

Phase2ë¡œ ë„˜ì–´ê°‘ì‹œë‹¤

---

**Cursor**

Phase 2 ì‹œì‘ ì¤€ë¹„ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. Phase 2 ì‘ì—… ë²”ìœ„ë¥¼ í™•ì¸ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.


Phase 2 ì‹œì‘ ì¤€ë¹„ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. ì‘ì—… ë²”ìœ„ì™€ ìˆœì„œë¥¼ ì •ë¦¬ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.


## Phase 2 ì‹œì‘ ì¤€ë¹„

**ì‘ì—… ë²”ìœ„**: ë°±ì—”ë“œ íŒŒì„œ êµ¬í˜„ (ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì‹±)

### ì‘ì—… ëª©ë¡

1. **ê¸°ë³¸ ë°ì´í„° ëª¨ë¸ ì •ì˜** (`backend/core/models.py`)
   - íŒŒì„œì— í•„ìš”í•œ ìµœì†Œ ëª¨ë¸ ì •ì˜ (SessionMeta, Turn, CodeBlock)
   - Phase 3ì—ì„œ í™•ì¥ ì˜ˆì •

2. **í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì •ê·œí™”** (`backend/parser/normalize.py`)
   - ì¤„ë°”ê¿ˆ í†µì¼, BOM ì œê±°, ê³µë°± ì •ë¦¬

3. **ì„¸ì…˜ ë©”íƒ€ ì¶”ì¶œ** (`backend/parser/meta.py`)
   - Phase, Subphase, Exported at, Cursor version ì¶”ì¶œ

4. **Turn ë¸”ë¡ íŒŒì‹±** (`backend/parser/turns.py`)
   - êµ¬ë¶„ì„  ê¸°ì¤€ ë¶„í• , Speaker ì¶”ì¶œ, Fallback íŒŒì„œ

5. **ì½”ë“œ ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ** (`backend/parser/snippets.py`)
   - ì½”ë“œíœìŠ¤ ì¶”ì¶œ, ì–¸ì–´ íŒë³„

6. **Artifact ì¶”ì¶œ** (`backend/parser/artifacts.py`)
   - íŒŒì¼/ê²½ë¡œ í›„ë³´ ì¶”ì¶œ, íƒ€ì… ë¶„ë¥˜

7. **íŒŒì„œ í†µí•©** (`backend/parser/__init__.py`)
   - ì „ì²´ íŒŒì‹± íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ í†µí•©

8. **í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‘ì„±**
   - ë‹¨ìœ„ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ (`tests/test_parser.py`)
   - E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ (`tests/test_parser_e2e.py`)

**ì˜ˆìƒ ì‹œê°„**: ì•½ 2-3ì‹œê°„  
**ì˜ì¡´ì„±**: Phase 1 ì™„ë£Œ

### ì‘ì—… ìˆœì„œ ì œì•ˆ

1. ê¸°ë³¸ ë°ì´í„° ëª¨ë¸ ì •ì˜ (íŒŒì„œ ë™ì‘ì— í•„ìˆ˜)
2. íŒŒì„œ ëª¨ë“ˆ êµ¬í˜„ (normalize â†’ meta â†’ turns â†’ snippets â†’ artifacts)
3. íŒŒì„œ í†µí•© ë° í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸

ì´ ìˆœì„œë¡œ ì§„í–‰í• ê¹Œìš”, ì•„ë‹ˆë©´ ë‹¤ë¥¸ ìˆœì„œë¥¼ ì›í•˜ì‹œë‚˜ìš”?

---

**User**

ë„¤ ìˆœì„œëŒ€ë¡œ ì§„í–‰

---

**Cursor**

Phase 2 ì‘ì—…ì„ ìˆœì„œëŒ€ë¡œ ì§„í–‰í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤. ë¨¼ì € ê¸°ë³¸ ë°ì´í„° ëª¨ë¸ì„ ì •ì˜í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.


íŒŒì„œì— í•„ìš”í•œ ê¸°ë³¸ ë°ì´í„° ëª¨ë¸ ì •ì˜ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.


```python
"""
ë°ì´í„° ëª¨ë¸ ì •ì˜

ì´ ëª¨ë“ˆì€ íŒŒì„œ, ë¹Œë”, APIì—ì„œ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ëŠ” Pydantic ëª¨ë¸ì„ ì •ì˜í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
"""

from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import Optional, List


class SessionMeta(BaseModel):
    """ì„¸ì…˜ ë©”íƒ€ë°ì´í„°"""

    session_id: str
    exported_at: Optional[str] = None
    cursor_version: Optional[str] = None
    phase: Optional[int] = None
    subphase: Optional[int] = None
    source_doc: str


class CodeBlock(BaseModel):
    """ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡"""

    block_index: int
    lang: str  # ì–¸ì–´ (ë¹ˆ ë¬¸ìì—´ ê°€ëŠ¥)
    code: str  # ì½”ë“œ ë‚´ìš©


class Turn(BaseModel):
    """Turn ë¸”ë¡ (User/Cursor ëŒ€í™” ë‹¨ìœ„)"""

    turn_index: int
    speaker: str  # "User", "Cursor", "Unknown"
    body: str  # ë³¸ë¬¸ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ (ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ ì œì™¸)
    code_blocks: List[CodeBlock] = []  # ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸
    path_candidates: List[str] = []  # íŒŒì¼/ê²½ë¡œ í›„ë³´ ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸

```

ê¸°ë³¸ ë°ì´í„° ëª¨ë¸ ì •ì˜ ì™„ë£Œ. í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì •ê·œí™” ëª¨ë“ˆ êµ¬í˜„ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.


```python
"""
í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì •ê·œí™” ëª¨ë“ˆ

ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì¼ì˜ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ë¥¼ ì •ê·œí™”í•˜ì—¬ íŒŒì‹±í•˜ê¸° ì‰½ê²Œ ë§Œë“­ë‹ˆë‹¤.
"""

import re


def normalize_text(text: str, preserve_code_blocks: bool = True) -> str:
    """
    í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì •ê·œí™”

    Args:
        text: ì›ë³¸ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸
        preserve_code_blocks: ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ ë‚´ë¶€ ë³´ì¡´ ì—¬ë¶€

    Returns:
        ì •ê·œí™”ëœ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # 1. ì¤„ë°”ê¿ˆ í†µì¼
    text = text.replace("\r\n", "\n").replace("\r", "\n")

    # 2. BOM ì œê±°
    text = text.lstrip("\ufeff")

    if preserve_code_blocks:
        # ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ ë¶„ë¦¬
        code_blocks = []
        pattern = r"```([a-zA-Z0-9_+-]+)?\n(.*?)```"

        def replace_code(match):
            idx = len(code_blocks)
            code_blocks.append(match.group(0))
            return f"__CODE_BLOCK_{idx}__"

        text = re.sub(pattern, replace_code, text, flags=re.DOTALL)

    # 3. íŠ¸ë ˆì¼ë§ ê³µë°± ì œê±°
    text = re.sub(r"[ \t]+$", "", text, flags=re.MULTILINE)

    # 4. ë„ˆë¬´ ê¸´ ê³µë°± ì¶•ì†Œ (3ê°œ ì´ìƒ â†’ 2ê°œ)
    text = re.sub(r" {3,}", "  ", text)

    if preserve_code_blocks:
        # ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ ë³µì›
        for idx, code in enumerate(code_blocks):
            text = text.replace(f"__CODE_BLOCK_{idx}__", code)

    return text

```

ì„¸ì…˜ ë©”íƒ€ ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“ˆ êµ¬í˜„ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.


```python
"""
ì„¸ì…˜ ë©”íƒ€ë°ì´í„° ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“ˆ

ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì¼ì—ì„œ ì„¸ì…˜ ë©”íƒ€ë°ì´í„°(Phase, Subphase, Exported at, Cursor version)ë¥¼ ì¶”ì¶œí•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
"""

import re
from typing import Optional
from backend.core.models import SessionMeta


# ì •ê·œì‹ íŒ¨í„´
EXPORTED_AT_RE = re.compile(
    r"(?i)Exported\s+(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}[^,\n]*?(?:KST|UTC|GMT|[+\-]\d{2}:\d{2})?)",
    re.MULTILINE,
)

CURSOR_VERSION_RE = re.compile(
    r"(?i)\bCursor\s+(\d+\.\d+\.\d+)\b",
    re.MULTILINE,
)

PHASE_RE = re.compile(
    r"(?i)\bPhase\s+(\d+)\b",
    re.MULTILINE,
)

SUBPHASE_RE = re.compile(
    r"(?i)\bSub\s*Phase\s+(\d+)\b",
    re.MULTILINE,
)


def extract_session_meta(text: str, source_doc: str) -> SessionMeta:
    """
    ìƒë‹¨ 2000~4000 chars ë²”ìœ„ì—ì„œ best-effortë¡œ ë©”íƒ€ ì¶”ì¶œ

    Args:
        text: ì›ë³¸ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸
        source_doc: ì†ŒìŠ¤ ë¬¸ì„œ ê²½ë¡œ

    Returns:
        SessionMeta ê°ì²´
    """
    # ìƒë‹¨ ë²”ìœ„ ì¶”ì¶œ
    header_text = text[:4000]

    # exported_at ì¶”ì¶œ
    exported_at_match = EXPORTED_AT_RE.search(header_text)
    exported_at = exported_at_match.group(1) if exported_at_match else None

    # cursor_version ì¶”ì¶œ
    version_match = CURSOR_VERSION_RE.search(header_text)
    cursor_version = version_match.group(1) if version_match else None

    # phase ì¶”ì¶œ
    phase_match = PHASE_RE.search(header_text)
    phase = int(phase_match.group(1)) if phase_match else None

    # subphase ì¶”ì¶œ
    subphase_match = SUBPHASE_RE.search(header_text)
    subphase = int(subphase_match.group(1)) if subphase_match else None

    # session_id ìƒì„±
    if exported_at:
        # ë¬¸ìì—´ ì •ê·œí™”: ê³µë°± â†’ _, : ì œê±°
        session_id_base = exported_at.replace(" ", "_").replace(":", "")
        session_id = f"cursor_export_{session_id_base}"
    else:
        session_id = f"cursor_export_unknown_{hash(text) % 10000}"

    return SessionMeta(
        session_id=session_id,
        exported_at=exported_at,
        cursor_version=cursor_version,
        phase=phase,
        subphase=subphase,
        source_doc=source_doc,
    )

```

ì½”ë“œ ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“ˆ êµ¬í˜„ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.


```python
"""
ì½”ë“œ ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“ˆ

ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì¼ì—ì„œ ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ì„ ì¶”ì¶œí•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
"""

import re
from typing import List
from backend.core.models import CodeBlock


CODE_FENCE_RE = re.compile(
    r"```([a-zA-Z0-9_+-]+)?\n(.*?)```",
    re.DOTALL,
)


def extract_code_blocks(text: str) -> List[CodeBlock]:
    """
    ì½”ë“œ íœìŠ¤ ì¶”ì¶œ

    Args:
        text: í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸

    Returns:
        CodeBlock ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    blocks = []
    matches = CODE_FENCE_RE.finditer(text)

    for idx, match in enumerate(matches):
        lang = (match.group(1) or "").lower()
        code = match.group(2)

        blocks.append(
            CodeBlock(
                block_index=idx,
                lang=lang,
                code=code,
            )
        )

    return blocks

```

Artifact ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“ˆ êµ¬í˜„ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.


```python
"""
Artifact ì¶”ì¶œ ëª¨ë“ˆ

ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì¼ì—ì„œ íŒŒì¼/ê²½ë¡œ í›„ë³´ë¥¼ ì¶”ì¶œí•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
"""

import re
from typing import List


# íŒŒì¼ ê²½ë¡œ íŒ¨í„´ (ë³´ìˆ˜ì )
PATH_RE = re.compile(
    r"(?:(?:[\w.-]+[/\\])+[\w.-]+\.(?:md|mdc|py|ts|tsx|sql|json)|"
    r"TODOs\.md|[\w.-]+\.(?:md|mdc|py|ts|tsx|sql|json))",
    re.IGNORECASE,
)


def extract_path_candidates(text: str) -> List[str]:
    """
    íŒŒì¼/ê²½ë¡œ í›„ë³´ ì¶”ì¶œ

    Args:
        text: í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸

    Returns:
        ê²½ë¡œ í›„ë³´ ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸ (ì¤‘ë³µ ì œê±°)
    """
    matches = PATH_RE.findall(text)
    # ì¤‘ë³µ ì œê±° ë° ì •ê·œí™”
    candidates = list(set(matches))
    return candidates

```

Turn ë¸”ë¡ íŒŒì‹± ëª¨ë“ˆ êµ¬í˜„ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.


```python
"""
Turn ë¸”ë¡ íŒŒì‹± ëª¨ë“ˆ

ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì¼ì„ Turn ë¸”ë¡ìœ¼ë¡œ ë¶„í• í•˜ê³  íŒŒì‹±í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
"""

import re
from typing import List
from backend.core.models import Turn
from backend.parser.snippets import extract_code_blocks
from backend.parser.artifacts import extract_path_candidates


# êµ¬ë¶„ì„  íŒ¨í„´
TURN_SPLIT_RE = re.compile(r"^\s*---\s*$", re.MULTILINE)

# Speaker ë¼ë²¨ íŒ¨í„´
SPEAKER_RE = re.compile(
    r"^\s*\*\*(User|Cursor)\*\*\s*:?\s*$",
    re.MULTILINE,
)

# Fallback: êµµê²Œ ëˆ„ë½ëœ ê²½ìš°
SPEAKER_FALLBACK_RE = re.compile(
    r"^\s*(User|Cursor)\s*:?\s*$",
    re.MULTILINE,
)


def split_to_turns(text: str) -> List[str]:
    """
    êµ¬ë¶„ì„  ê¸°ì¤€ìœ¼ë¡œ Turn ë¸”ë¡ ë¶„í• 

    Args:
        text: ì •ê·œí™”ëœ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸

    Returns:
        Turn ë¸”ë¡ ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # 1ì°¨: êµ¬ë¶„ì„  ê¸°ì¤€ ë¶„í• 
    blocks = TURN_SPLIT_RE.split(text)
    blocks = [b.strip() for b in blocks if b.strip()]

    # êµ¬ë¶„ì„ ì´ ì—†ê±°ë‚˜ ë„ˆë¬´ ì ìœ¼ë©´ fallback
    if len(blocks) < 2:
        return fallback_split_by_speaker(text)

    return blocks


def fallback_split_by_speaker(text: str) -> List[str]:
    """
    Speaker ë¼ë²¨ ê¸°ì¤€ìœ¼ë¡œ ë¶„í•  (fallback)
    """
    turns = []
    current_turn = []
    current_speaker = None

    for line in text.split("\n"):
        speaker_match = SPEAKER_RE.match(line) or SPEAKER_FALLBACK_RE.match(line)

        if speaker_match:
            # ìƒˆ Turn ì‹œì‘
            if current_turn:
                turns.append("\n".join(current_turn))
            current_speaker = speaker_match.group(1)
            current_turn = [line]
        else:
            current_turn.append(line)

    if current_turn:
        turns.append("\n".join(current_turn))

    return turns


def parse_turn(block: str, turn_index: int) -> Turn:
    """
    Turn ë¸”ë¡ íŒŒì‹±

    Args:
        block: Turn ë¸”ë¡ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸
        turn_index: Turn ì¸ë±ìŠ¤

    Returns:
        Turn ê°ì²´
    """
    # Speaker ì¶”ì¶œ
    speaker_match = SPEAKER_RE.search(block) or SPEAKER_FALLBACK_RE.search(block)
    speaker = speaker_match.group(1) if speaker_match else "Unknown"

    # ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ ì œê±°í•œ body ì¶”ì¶œ
    body = re.sub(r"```.*?```", "", block, flags=re.DOTALL)
    body = re.sub(r"^\s*\*\*(User|Cursor)\*\*\s*:?\s*", "", body, flags=re.MULTILINE)
    body = body.strip()

    # ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ ì¶”ì¶œ
    code_blocks = extract_code_blocks(block)

    # íŒŒì¼ ê²½ë¡œ í›„ë³´ ì¶”ì¶œ
    path_candidates = extract_path_candidates(block)

    return Turn(
        turn_index=turn_index,
        speaker=speaker,
        body=body,
        code_blocks=code_blocks,
        path_candidates=path_candidates,
    )


def check_parse_health(turns: List[Turn]) -> dict:
    """
    íŒŒì‹± í’ˆì§ˆ ê²€ì‚¬

    Args:
        turns: Turn ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸

    Returns:
        {
            "unknown_ratio": float,
            "warnings": List[str]
        }
    """
    total = len(turns)
    unknown_count = sum(1 for t in turns if t.speaker == "Unknown")
    unknown_ratio = unknown_count / total if total > 0 else 0.0

    warnings = []
    if unknown_ratio > 0.2:
        warnings.append(
            f"High Unknown speaker ratio: {unknown_ratio:.1%}. "
            "Format detection may have failed."
        )

    return {
        "unknown_ratio": unknown_ratio,
        "warnings": warnings,
    }

```

íŒŒì„œ í†µí•© ëª¨ë“ˆ êµ¬í˜„ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.


```python
"""
ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì„œ ëª¨ë“ˆ

Cursor IDE export ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì¼ì„ êµ¬ì¡°í™”ëœ ë°ì´í„°ë¡œ íŒŒì‹±í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
"""

from backend.parser.normalize import normalize_text
from backend.parser.meta import extract_session_meta
from backend.parser.turns import split_to_turns, parse_turn, check_parse_health
from backend.core.models import SessionMeta, Turn, CodeBlock
from typing import Dict, List


def parse_markdown(text: str, source_doc: str = "input.md") -> Dict:
    """
    ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì¼ ì „ì²´ íŒŒì‹±

    Args:
        text: ë§ˆí¬ë‹¤ìš´ íŒŒì¼ ë‚´ìš©
        source_doc: ì†ŒìŠ¤ ë¬¸ì„œ ê²½ë¡œ

    Returns:
        {
            "session_meta": SessionMeta,
            "turns": List[Turn],
            "code_blocks": List[CodeBlock],
            "artifacts": List[str]
        }
    """
    # 1. ì •ê·œí™”
    normalized = normalize_text(text)

    # 2. ë©”íƒ€ ì¶”ì¶œ
    session_meta = extract_session_meta(normalized, source_doc)

    # 3. Turn ë¶„í• 
    turn_blocks = split_to_turns(normalized)

    # 4. Turn íŒŒì‹±
    turns = []
    for idx, block in enumerate(turn_blocks):
        turn = parse_turn(block, idx)
        turns.append(turn)

    # 5. ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ ìˆ˜ì§‘
    all_code_blocks = []
    for turn in turns:
        all_code_blocks.extend(turn.code_blocks)

    # 6. Artifact ìˆ˜ì§‘
    all_paths = []
    for turn in turns:
        all_paths.extend(turn.path_candidates)

    return {
        "session_meta": session_meta,
        "turns": turns,
        "code_blocks": all_code_blocks,
        "artifacts": list(set(all_paths)),
    }

```

íŒŒì„œ êµ¬í˜„ ì™„ë£Œ. ê¸°ë³¸ ë™ì‘ í™•ì¸ì„ ìœ„í•œ ë‹¨ìœ„ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‘ì„± ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.


```python
"""
íŒŒì„œ ë‹¨ìœ„ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸

ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì—¬ íŒŒì„œ ëª¨ë“ˆì„ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
"""

import pytest
from pathlib import Path
from backend.parser import parse_markdown, normalize_text
from backend.parser.meta import extract_session_meta
from backend.parser.turns import split_to_turns, parse_turn, check_parse_health
from backend.parser.snippets import extract_code_blocks
from backend.parser.artifacts import extract_path_candidates


# ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„° ê²½ë¡œ
FIXTURE_DIR = Path(__file__).parent / "fixtures"
INPUT_FILE = FIXTURE_DIR / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"


def test_normalize():
    """ì •ê·œí™” í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ (ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©)"""
    if not INPUT_FILE.exists():
        pytest.skip(f"Input file not found: {INPUT_FILE}")

    text = INPUT_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

    # ì •ê·œí™” ì‹¤í–‰
    normalized = normalize_text(text)

    # ê²€ì¦
    assert "\r\n" not in normalized, "ì¤„ë°”ê¿ˆì´ í†µì¼ë˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ"
    assert "\r" not in normalized, "ì¤„ë°”ê¿ˆì´ í†µì¼ë˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ"
    assert not normalized.startswith("\ufeff"), "BOMì´ ì œê±°ë˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ"


def test_meta_extraction():
    """ë©”íƒ€ ì¶”ì¶œ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ (ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©)"""
    if not INPUT_FILE.exists():
        pytest.skip(f"Input file not found: {INPUT_FILE}")

    text = INPUT_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

    # ë©”íƒ€ ì¶”ì¶œ ì‹¤í–‰
    session_meta = extract_session_meta(text, str(INPUT_FILE))

    # ê²€ì¦
    assert session_meta.session_id is not None, "session_idê°€ ìƒì„±ë˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ"
    assert session_meta.source_doc == str(INPUT_FILE), "source_docê°€ ì˜¬ë°”ë¥´ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ"
    # phase, subphase, exported_at, cursor_versionì€ ìˆì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìŒ


def test_turn_parsing():
    """Turn íŒŒì‹± í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ (ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©)"""
    if not INPUT_FILE.exists():
        pytest.skip(f"Input file not found: {INPUT_FILE}")

    text = INPUT_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    normalized = normalize_text(text)

    # Turn ë¶„í•  ì‹¤í–‰
    turn_blocks = split_to_turns(normalized)

    # ê²€ì¦
    assert len(turn_blocks) > 0, "Turn ë¸”ë¡ì´ ë¶„í• ë˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ"

    # Turn íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤í–‰
    turns = []
    for idx, block in enumerate(turn_blocks):
        turn = parse_turn(block, idx)
        turns.append(turn)

    # ê²€ì¦
    assert len(turns) > 0, "Turnì´ íŒŒì‹±ë˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ"

    # Parse Health Check
    health = check_parse_health(turns)
    assert health["unknown_ratio"] < 0.2, f"Unknown speaker ë¹„ìœ¨ì´ ë„ˆë¬´ ë†’ìŒ: {health['unknown_ratio']:.1%}"


def test_snippet_extraction():
    """ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ (ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©)"""
    if not INPUT_FILE.exists():
        pytest.skip(f"Input file not found: {INPUT_FILE}")

    text = INPUT_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

    # ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ ì‹¤í–‰
    code_blocks = extract_code_blocks(text)

    # ê²€ì¦ (ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ì´ ìˆì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìŒ)
    # ìµœì†Œí•œ í•¨ìˆ˜ê°€ ì •ìƒ ë™ì‘í•˜ëŠ”ì§€ í™•ì¸
    assert isinstance(code_blocks, list), "ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ì´ ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸ê°€ ì•„ë‹˜"


def test_artifact_extraction():
    """Artifact ì¶”ì¶œ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ (ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©)"""
    if not INPUT_FILE.exists():
        pytest.skip(f"Input file not found: {INPUT_FILE}")

    text = INPUT_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

    # Artifact ì¶”ì¶œ ì‹¤í–‰
    path_candidates = extract_path_candidates(text)

    # ê²€ì¦ (ê²½ë¡œ í›„ë³´ê°€ ìˆì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìŒ)
    # ìµœì†Œí•œ í•¨ìˆ˜ê°€ ì •ìƒ ë™ì‘í•˜ëŠ”ì§€ í™•ì¸
    assert isinstance(path_candidates, list), "ê²½ë¡œ í›„ë³´ê°€ ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸ê°€ ì•„ë‹˜"


def test_parse_markdown_full():
    """ì „ì²´ íŒŒì‹± íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ (ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©)"""
    if not INPUT_FILE.exists():
        pytest.skip(f"Input file not found: {INPUT_FILE}")

    text = INPUT_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

    # ì „ì²´ íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤í–‰
    result = parse_markdown(text, str(INPUT_FILE))

    # ê²€ì¦
    assert "session_meta" in result, "session_metaê°€ ì—†ìŒ"
    assert "turns" in result, "turnsê°€ ì—†ìŒ"
    assert "code_blocks" in result, "code_blocksê°€ ì—†ìŒ"
    assert "artifacts" in result, "artifactsê°€ ì—†ìŒ"

    assert result["session_meta"].session_id is not None, "session_idê°€ ì—†ìŒ"
    assert len(result["turns"]) > 0, "turnsê°€ ë¹„ì–´ìˆìŒ"

    # Parse Health Check
    health = check_parse_health(result["turns"])
    assert health["unknown_ratio"] < 0.2, f"Unknown speaker ë¹„ìœ¨ì´ ë„ˆë¬´ ë†’ìŒ: {health['unknown_ratio']:.1%}"

```

## Phase 2 íŒŒì„œ êµ¬í˜„ ì™„ë£Œ

### ì™„ë£Œëœ ì‘ì—…

1. **ê¸°ë³¸ ë°ì´í„° ëª¨ë¸ ì •ì˜** (`backend/core/models.py`)
   - `SessionMeta`: ì„¸ì…˜ ë©”íƒ€ë°ì´í„°
   - `CodeBlock`: ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡
   - `Turn`: Turn ë¸”ë¡ (User/Cursor ëŒ€í™” ë‹¨ìœ„)

2. **í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì •ê·œí™”** (`backend/parser/normalize.py`)
   - ì¤„ë°”ê¿ˆ í†µì¼, BOM ì œê±°, ê³µë°± ì •ë¦¬

3. **ì„¸ì…˜ ë©”íƒ€ ì¶”ì¶œ** (`backend/parser/meta.py`)
   - Phase, Subphase, Exported at, Cursor version ì¶”ì¶œ

4. **ì½”ë“œ ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ** (`backend/parser/snippets.py`)
   - ì½”ë“œíœìŠ¤ ì¶”ì¶œ, ì–¸ì–´ íŒë³„

5. **Artifact ì¶”ì¶œ** (`backend/parser/artifacts.py`)
   - íŒŒì¼/ê²½ë¡œ í›„ë³´ ì¶”ì¶œ

6. **Turn ë¸”ë¡ íŒŒì‹±** (`backend/parser/turns.py`)
   - êµ¬ë¶„ì„  ê¸°ì¤€ ë¶„í• , Speaker ì¶”ì¶œ, Fallback íŒŒì„œ, Parse Health Check

7. **íŒŒì„œ í†µí•©** (`backend/parser/__init__.py`)
   - ì „ì²´ íŒŒì‹± íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ í†µí•©

8. **ë‹¨ìœ„ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‘ì„±** (`tests/test_parser.py`)
   - ê° ëª¨ë“ˆë³„ ë‹¨ìœ„ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ (ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©)

### ë‹¤ìŒ ë‹¨ê³„

1. í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ (ì„ íƒ)
   - `poetry run pytest tests/test_parser.py -v`ë¡œ íŒŒì„œ ë™ì‘ í™•ì¸

2. E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‘ì„±
   - `tests/test_parser_e2e.py` ì‘ì„± (Phase 2 ì™„ë£Œ ê²€ì¦ìš©)

3. TODOs.md ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸
   - Phase 2 ì™„ë£Œ í•­ëª© ì²´í¬

í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ë¥¼ ì‹¤í–‰í•´ í™•ì¸í• ê¹Œìš”, ì•„ë‹ˆë©´ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‘ì„±ë¶€í„° ì§„í–‰í• ê¹Œìš”?

---

**User**

e2e ë°”ë¡œ ì‹¤ì‹œ

---

**Cursor**

E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‘ì„± ë° ì‹¤í–‰ ì§„í–‰í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.


```python
"""
íŒŒì„œ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸

ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°ë¡œ ì „ì²´ íŒŒì„œ íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ì„ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
"""

import pytest
import json
from pathlib import Path
from backend.parser import parse_markdown
from backend.parser.turns import check_parse_health


# ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„° ê²½ë¡œ
INPUT_FILE = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
REPORT_DIR = Path(__file__).parent / "reports"
REPORT_FILE = REPORT_DIR / "parser_e2e_report.json"


def test_parser_e2e():
    """
    ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°ë¡œ ì „ì²´ íŒŒì„œ íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # 1. ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„° ë¡œë“œ
    if not INPUT_FILE.exists():
        pytest.skip(f"Input file not found: {INPUT_FILE}")

    text = INPUT_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

    # 2. íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤í–‰
    result = parse_markdown(text, source_doc=str(INPUT_FILE))

    # 3. ì •í•©ì„± ê²€ì¦
    assert result["session_meta"] is not None, "session_metaê°€ ì—†ìŒ"
    assert result["session_meta"].session_id is not None, "session_idê°€ ì—†ìŒ"
    assert len(result["turns"]) > 0, "turnsê°€ ë¹„ì–´ìˆìŒ"

    # Session Meta ì¶”ì¶œ ì •í™•ì„±
    session_meta = result["session_meta"]
    assert session_meta.source_doc == str(INPUT_FILE), "source_docê°€ ì˜¬ë°”ë¥´ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ"
    # phase, subphase, exported_at, cursor_versionì€ ìˆì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìŒ

    # Turn ë¸”ë¡ ë¶„í•  ì •í™•ì„±
    user_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "User"]
    cursor_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "Cursor"]
    unknown_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "Unknown"]

    assert len(user_turns) > 0, "User turnsê°€ ì—†ìŒ"
    assert len(cursor_turns) > 0, "Cursor turnsê°€ ì—†ìŒ"

    # ì½”ë“œ ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ ì •í™•ì„±
    all_code_blocks = result["code_blocks"]
    # ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ì´ ìˆì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìŒ

    # Artifact ì¶”ì¶œ ì •í™•ì„±
    all_artifacts = result["artifacts"]
    # Artifactê°€ ìˆì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìŒ

    # 4. íƒ€ë‹¹ì„± ê²€ì¦
    # íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤íŒ¨ìœ¨ ê²€ì¦
    health = check_parse_health(result["turns"])
    unknown_ratio = health["unknown_ratio"]

    assert unknown_ratio < 0.2, f"íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤íŒ¨ìœ¨ì´ ë„ˆë¬´ ë†’ìŒ: {unknown_ratio:.1%}"

    # 5. ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„ ë° ìë™ ë³´ê³ 
    report = {
        "test_name": "parser_e2e",
        "input_file": str(INPUT_FILE),
        "results": {
            "total_turns": len(result["turns"]),
            "user_turns": len(user_turns),
            "cursor_turns": len(cursor_turns),
            "unknown_turns": len(unknown_turns),
            "unknown_ratio": unknown_ratio,
            "code_blocks": len(all_code_blocks),
            "artifacts": len(all_artifacts),
            "session_meta": {
                "session_id": session_meta.session_id,
                "exported_at": session_meta.exported_at,
                "cursor_version": session_meta.cursor_version,
                "phase": session_meta.phase,
                "subphase": session_meta.subphase,
            },
        },
        "warnings": health.get("warnings", []),
        "errors": [],
        "status": "PASS" if unknown_ratio < 0.2 else "WARNING",
    }

    # ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ì¶œë ¥
    print("\n" + "=" * 50)
    print("Parser E2E Test Report")
    print("=" * 50)
    print(json.dumps(report, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
    print("=" * 50)

    # ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥
    REPORT_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    REPORT_FILE.write_text(
        json.dumps(report, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    # ìµœì¢… ê²€ì¦
    assert unknown_ratio < 0.2, f"Unknown speaker ë¹„ìœ¨ì´ ë„ˆë¬´ ë†’ìŒ: {unknown_ratio:.1%}"

```

E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.


E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ í†µê³¼. ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ í™•ì¸ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.

## E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë°©ì‹ ê²€í†  ê²°ê³¼

### 1. ë°±ì—”ë“œ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ì˜ ì‹¤íš¨ì„± ê²€í† 

í˜„ì¬ ìƒí™©:
- Phase 2: íŒŒì„œ ëª¨ë“ˆ ì§ì ‘ í˜¸ì¶œ (ì„œë²„ ë¶ˆí•„ìš”)
- Phase 6 ì´í›„: API ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ (ì„œë²„ í•„ìš”)

ê²€í†  ê²°ê³¼:

ì¥ì :
- Phase 6 ì´í›„: API í†µí•© ê²€ì¦ì— í•„ìˆ˜
- í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ í”Œë¡œìš°ì™€ ë™ì¼í•œ ê²€ì¦
- HTTP ë ˆë²¨ ì—ëŸ¬ ì²˜ë¦¬ ê²€ì¦ ê°€ëŠ¥

ë‹¨ì :
- Phase 2-5: ì„œë²„ê°€ ì—†ì–´ ë¶ˆí•„ìš”
- ì„œë²„ ì‹œì‘/ì¢…ë£Œë¡œ ì¸í•œ ì˜¤ë²„í—¤ë“œ
- í¬íŠ¸ ì¶©ëŒ ê°€ëŠ¥ì„±

ê¶Œì¥ì‚¬í•­:
- Phaseë³„ êµ¬ë¶„ ì ìš©
  - Phase 2-5: ëª¨ë“ˆ ì§ì ‘ í˜¸ì¶œ (ì„œë²„ ë¶ˆí•„ìš”)
  - Phase 6 ì´í›„: ì‹¤ì œ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ (API í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ í•„ìˆ˜)
- `conftest_e2e.py`ì—ì„œ Phaseë³„ fixture ë¶„ë¦¬
  - `test_server` fixtureëŠ” Phase 6+ì—ì„œë§Œ ì‚¬ìš©
  - Phase 2-5ëŠ” ëª¨ë“ˆ ì§ì ‘ í˜¸ì¶œ

### 2. ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥ (í•„ìˆ˜)

í˜„ì¬ ìƒí™©:
- `testing-strategy.mdc`ì— ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥ íŒ¨í„´ì€ ìˆìœ¼ë‚˜ í•„ìˆ˜ ì•„ë‹˜
- ì‹¤ì œ êµ¬í˜„ì€ ì—†ìŒ

ê²€í†  ê²°ê³¼:

í•„ìš”ì„±:
- ë””ë²„ê¹…ì— ìœ ìš©
- í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ ì¶”ì  ê°€ëŠ¥
- ì˜¤ë¥˜ ì›ì¸ ë¶„ì„ì— ë„ì›€

ê¶Œì¥ì‚¬í•­:
- í•„ìˆ˜ë¡œ ì§€ì •
- ì €ì¥ ìœ„ì¹˜: `tests/logs/test_{test_name}_{timestamp}.log`
- ë¡œê·¸ ë ˆë²¨: DEBUG (ìƒì„¸ ì •ë³´ í¬í•¨)
- í˜•ì‹: íƒ€ì„ìŠ¤íƒ¬í”„, ë¡œê·¸ ë ˆë²¨, ë©”ì‹œì§€

êµ¬í˜„ ì˜ˆì‹œ:
```python
# conftest_e2e.pyì— ì¶”ê°€
import logging
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime

@pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
def setup_test_logging(request):
    """ëª¨ë“  E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ì— ìë™ìœ¼ë¡œ ë¡œê¹… ì„¤ì •"""
    log_dir = Path(__file__).parent / "logs"
    log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
    test_name = request.node.name
    log_file = log_dir / f"{test_name}_{timestamp}.log"
    
    logging.basicConfig(
        level=logging.DEBUG,
        format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
        handlers=[
            logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding='utf-8'),
            logging.StreamHandler()
        ]
    )
    
    yield
    
    # í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì¢…ë£Œ í›„ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ê²½ë¡œ ì¶œë ¥
    print(f"\n[LOG] Test log saved to: {log_file}")
```

### 3. ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼ ì €ì¥ (í•„ìˆ˜)

í˜„ì¬ ìƒí™©:
- ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼(`parser_e2e_report.json`)ì€ ì €ì¥ë˜ì§€ë§Œ ìš”ì•½ë§Œ í¬í•¨
- ìƒì„¸ íŒŒì‹± ê²°ê³¼(Turn ë‚´ìš©, ì½”ë“œ ë¸”ë¡ ë“±)ëŠ” ì €ì¥ë˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ

ê²€í†  ê²°ê³¼:

í•„ìš”ì„±:
- ì‚¬ìš©ì ë¦¬ë·° ë° í”¼ë“œë°±ì— í•„ìš”
- íšŒê·€ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë¹„êµì— ìœ ìš©
- ê²°ê³¼ ê²€ì¦ ë° ë””ë²„ê¹…ì— ë„ì›€

ê¶Œì¥ì‚¬í•­:
- í•„ìˆ˜ë¡œ ì§€ì •
- ì €ì¥ ìœ„ì¹˜: `tests/results/{test_name}_{timestamp}.json`
- ì €ì¥ ë‚´ìš©:
  - íŒŒì‹± ê²°ê³¼ ì „ì²´ (SessionMeta, Turns, CodeBlocks, Artifacts)
  - ì´ë²¤íŠ¸ ì¶”ì¶œ ê²°ê³¼ (Phase 3 ì´í›„)
  - Timeline/Issues ìƒì„± ê²°ê³¼ (Phase 4 ì´í›„)
- íŒŒì¼ í¬ê¸° ê³ ë ¤: ëŒ€ìš©ëŸ‰ ê²°ê³¼ëŠ” ì••ì¶• ë˜ëŠ” ì„ íƒì  ì €ì¥

êµ¬í˜„ ì˜ˆì‹œ:
```python
# test_parser_e2e.pyì— ì¶”ê°€
from datetime import datetime

def test_parser_e2e():
    # ... í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ ...
    
    # ìƒì„¸ ê²°ê³¼ ì €ì¥
    results_dir = Path(__file__).parent / "results"
    results_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
    results_file = results_dir / f"parser_e2e_{timestamp}.json"
    
    # Pydantic ëª¨ë¸ì„ dictë¡œ ë³€í™˜í•˜ì—¬ ì €ì¥
    detailed_results = {
        "session_meta": result["session_meta"].dict(),
        "turns": [turn.dict() for turn in result["turns"]],
        "code_blocks": [block.dict() for block in result["code_blocks"]],
        "artifacts": result["artifacts"],
        "test_metadata": {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "input_file": str(INPUT_FILE),
        }
    }
    
    results_file.write_text(
        json.dumps(detailed_results, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False),
        encoding="utf-8"
    )
    
    print(f"\n[RESULTS] Detailed results saved to: {results_file}")
```

### ì¢…í•© ê¶Œì¥ì‚¬í•­

def setup_test_logging(request):
    """ëª¨ë“  E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ì— ìë™ìœ¼ë¡œ ë¡œê¹… ì„¤ì •"""

        level=logging.DEBUG,

            logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding='utf-8'),
            logging.StreamHandler()

    )

# Testing Strategy

## Overview
í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸ëŠ” E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì¤‘ì‹¬ì˜ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì „ëµì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤. Phaseë³„ë¡œ ì ì ˆí•œ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë°©ì‹ì„ ì„ íƒí•˜ì—¬ í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ í”Œë¡œìš°ì™€ ë™ì¼í•˜ê²Œ ê²€ì¦í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

## Domain Knowledge

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì›ì¹™
1. **E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ìš°ì„ **: ëª¨ë“  í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš© í•„ìˆ˜
2. **ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©**: Mock ì‚¬ìš© ì ˆëŒ€ ê¸ˆì§€
3. **í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ í”Œë¡œìš° ë™ì¼**: ë°°í¬ í›„ ë¬¸ì œê°€ ì—†ìŒì„ ë³´ì¥
4. **ìë™ ë³´ê³  í•„ìˆ˜**: í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ í›„ ìƒì„¸ ë¶„ì„ ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸
5. **ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥ í•„ìˆ˜**: ëª¨ë“  E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥ (ë””ë²„ê¹… í•„ìˆ˜)
6. **ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼ ì €ì¥ í•„ìˆ˜**: íŒŒì‹±/ì¶”ì¶œ ê²°ê³¼ë¥¼ ìƒì„¸íˆ ì €ì¥ (ì‚¬ìš©ì ë¦¬ë·°/í”¼ë“œë°± í•„ìˆ˜)

### Phaseë³„ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ êµ¬ë¶„
- **Phase 2-5**: ëª¨ë“ˆ ì§ì ‘ í˜¸ì¶œ (ì„œë²„ ë¶ˆí•„ìš”)
  - íŒŒì„œ, ì´ë²¤íŠ¸ ì •ê·œí™”, Timeline/Issues ë¹Œë” ë“±ì€ ëª¨ë“ˆ ì§ì ‘ í˜¸ì¶œ
  - ì„œë²„ ì‹œì‘ ì˜¤ë²„í—¤ë“œ ì—†ì´ ë¹ ë¥¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ê°€ëŠ¥
- **Phase 6+**: ì‹¤ì œ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ (API í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ í•„ìˆ˜)
  - API ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ì‹¤ì œ uvicorn ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ í•„ìˆ˜
  - HTTP ë ˆë²¨ í†µí•© ê²€ì¦ í•„ìš”

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°
- ì‹¤ì œ Cursor export íŒŒì¼: `docs/cursor_phase_6_3.md`
- ê° Phaseë³„ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ì—ì„œ ë™ì¼ íŒŒì¼ ì‚¬ìš©

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë‹¨ê³„ë³„ ê²€ì¦
- **ì •í•©ì„± ê²€ì¦**: êµ¬ì¡°ì  ì •í™•ì„± í™•ì¸
- **íƒ€ë‹¹ì„± ê²€ì¦**: ì‹¤ì œ ìƒí™©ì—ì„œì˜ í’ˆì§ˆ í™•ì¸
- **ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„**: ìƒì„¸ ë¶„ì„ ë° ê°œì„ ì  ë„ì¶œ

## Standards & Conventions

### 1. íŒŒì¼ êµ¬ì¡°
```
tests/
â”œâ”€â”€ fixtures/

### 2. E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ Fixture

```python
# tests/conftest_e2e.py
import pytest
import subprocess
import time
import httpx
from pathlib import Path

@pytest.fixture(scope="session")
def test_server():
    """
    ì‹¤ì œ uvicorn ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ fixture
    """
    # ì„œë²„ ì‹œì‘
    process = subprocess.Popen(
        ["poetry", "run", "uvicorn", "backend.main:app", "--host", "0.0.0.0", "--port", "8000"],
        cwd=Path(__file__).parent.parent,
        stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
        stderr=subprocess.PIPE
    )
    
    # ì„œë²„ ì¤€ë¹„ ëŒ€ê¸°
    max_retries = 30
    for _ in range(max_retries):
        try:
            response = httpx.get("http://localhost:8000/health", timeout=1.0)
            if response.status_code == 200:
                break
        except:
            time.sleep(0.5)
    else:
        process.terminate()
        raise RuntimeError("Server failed to start")
    
    yield process
    
    # ì„œë²„ ì¢…ë£Œ
    process.terminate()
    process.wait()

@pytest.fixture
def client(test_server):
    """
    httpx.Client fixture (ì‹¤ì œ HTTP ìš”ì²­)
    """
    return httpx.Client(base_url="http://localhost:8000", timeout=30.0)
```

### 3. E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ íŒ¨í„´

```python
# tests/test_parser_e2e.py
import pytest
from pathlib import Path
from backend.parser import parse_markdown

def test_parser_e2e():
    """
    ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°ë¡œ ì „ì²´ íŒŒì„œ íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # 1. ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„° ë¡œë“œ
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    text = input_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8')
    
    # 2. íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤í–‰
    result = parse_markdown(text, source_doc=str(input_file))
    
    # 3. ì •í•©ì„± ê²€ì¦
    assert result["session_meta"] is not None
    assert result["session_meta"].session_id is not None
    assert len(result["turns"]) > 0
    
    # Session Meta ì¶”ì¶œ ì •í™•ì„±
    assert result["session_meta"].phase is not None or result["session_meta"].phase is None
    # (phaseê°€ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìœ¼ë¯€ë¡œ Noneë„ í—ˆìš©)
    
    # Turn ë¸”ë¡ ë¶„í•  ì •í™•ì„±
    user_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "User"]
    cursor_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "Cursor"]
    unknown_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "Unknown"]
    
    assert len(user_turns) > 0, "User turns should exist"
    assert len(cursor_turns) > 0, "Cursor turns should exist"
    
    # Unknown ë¹„ìœ¨ ê²€ì¦
    unknown_ratio = len(unknown_turns) / len(result["turns"])
    assert unknown_ratio < 0.2, f"Unknown speaker ratio too high: {unknown_ratio:.1%}"
    
    # ì½”ë“œ ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ ì •í™•ì„±
    all_code_blocks = []
    for turn in result["turns"]:
        all_code_blocks.extend(turn.code_blocks)
    
    assert len(all_code_blocks) > 0, "Code blocks should be extracted"
    
    # 4. íƒ€ë‹¹ì„± ê²€ì¦
    # íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤íŒ¨ìœ¨ ê²€ì¦
    assert unknown_ratio < 0.2, "Parse failure rate too high"
    
    # 5. ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„ ë° í”¼ë“œë°±
    print(f"\n[Parser E2E Test Results]")
    print(f"Total turns: {len(result['turns'])}")
    print(f"User turns: {len(user_turns)}")
    print(f"Cursor turns: {len(cursor_turns)}")
    print(f"Unknown turns: {len(unknown_turns)} ({unknown_ratio:.1%})")
    print(f"Code blocks: {len(all_code_blocks)}")
    print(f"Artifacts: {len(result.get('artifacts', []))}")
```

### 4. API E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ íŒ¨í„´

```python
# tests/test_api_e2e.py
import pytest
from pathlib import Path
import httpx

def test_parse_endpoint_e2e(client: httpx.Client):
    """
    POST /api/parse ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ íŒŒì¼
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    
    with open(input_file, "rb") as f:
        files = {"file": ("cursor_phase_6_3.md", f, "text/markdown")}
        response = client.post("/api/parse", files=files)
    
    assert response.status_code == 200
    
    data = response.json()
    
    # ì‘ë‹µ ìŠ¤í‚¤ë§ˆ ê²€ì¦
    assert "session_meta" in data
    assert "turns" in data
    assert "events" in data
    
    # íŒŒì‹± ê²°ê³¼ ì •í™•ì„±
    assert data["session_meta"]["session_id"] is not None
    assert len(data["turns"]) > 0

def test_timeline_endpoint_e2e(client: httpx.Client):
    """
    POST /api/timeline ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # 1. ë¨¼ì € íŒŒì‹±
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    
    with open(input_file, "rb") as f:
        files = {"file": ("cursor_phase_6_3.md", f, "text/markdown")}
        parse_response = client.post("/api/parse", files=files)
    
    parse_data = parse_response.json()
    
    # 2. Timeline ìƒì„±
    timeline_response = client.post(
        "/api/timeline",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"],
            "events": parse_data["events"],
            "session_meta": parse_data["session_meta"]
        }
    )
    
    assert timeline_response.status_code == 200
    
    timeline_data = timeline_response.json()
    
    # Timeline JSON êµ¬ì¡° ê²€ì¦
    assert "session_meta" in timeline_data
    assert "timeline" in timeline_data
    assert len(timeline_data["timeline"]) > 0
    
    # Artifact/Snippet ì—°ê²° í™•ì¸
    for event in timeline_data["timeline"]:
        assert "seq" in event
        assert "type" in event
        assert "summary" in event
```

### 5. í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ í›„ ìë™ ë³´ê³ 

```python
# tests/test_parser_e2e.py
def test_parser_e2e_with_report():
    """
    í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ í›„ ìƒì„¸ ë³´ê³  í¬í•¨
    """
    # ... í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ ...
    
    # ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„
    report = {
        "test_name": "parser_e2e",
        "input_file": str(input_file),
        "results": {
            "total_turns": len(result["turns"]),
            "user_turns": len(user_turns),
            "cursor_turns": len(cursor_turns),
            "unknown_ratio": unknown_ratio,
            "code_blocks": len(all_code_blocks),
            "artifacts": len(result.get("artifacts", []))
        },
        "warnings": [],
        "errors": []
    }
    
    if unknown_ratio > 0.2:
        report["warnings"].append(
            f"High Unknown speaker ratio: {unknown_ratio:.1%}"
        )
    
    # ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ì¶œë ¥
    import json
    print("\n" + "="*50)
    print("E2E Test Report")
    print("="*50)
    print(json.dumps(report, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
    print("="*50)
    
    # ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥
    report_file = Path(__file__).parent / "reports" / "parser_e2e_report.json"
    report_file.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    report_file.write_text(
        json.dumps(report, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False),
        encoding='utf-8'
    )
```

## Implementation Patterns

### Pattern 1: Golden íŒŒì¼ ë¹„êµ

```python
# tests/test_parser_e2e.py
def test_parser_golden_comparison():
    """
    Golden íŒŒì¼ê³¼ ë¹„êµí•˜ì—¬ íšŒê·€ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # ì‹¤ì œ íŒŒì‹±
    result = parse_markdown(text, source_doc)
    
    # Golden íŒŒì¼ ë¡œë“œ
    golden_file = Path(__file__).parent / "golden" / "parser_expected.json"
    if golden_file.exists():
        expected = json.loads(golden_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
        
        # ë¹„êµ (ì£¼ìš” í•„ë“œë§Œ)
        assert result["session_meta"].session_id == expected["session_meta"]["session_id"]
        assert len(result["turns"]) == len(expected["turns"])
    else:
        # Golden íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„± (ìµœì´ˆ 1íšŒ)
        golden_file.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        golden_file.write_text(
            json.dumps({
                "session_meta": result["session_meta"].dict(),
                "turns_count": len(result["turns"])
            }, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False),
            encoding='utf-8'
        )
```

### Pattern 2: ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥

```python
# í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ ì‹œ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ë¡œ ì €ì¥
import logging
from pathlib import Path

def setup_test_logging():
    """
    í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ìš© ë¡œê¹… ì„¤ì •
    """
    log_dir = Path(__file__).parent / "logs"
    log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    
    log_file = log_dir / f"test_{time.strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.log"
    
    logging.basicConfig(
        level=logging.DEBUG,
        format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
        handlers=[
            logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding='utf-8'),
            logging.StreamHandler()
        ]
    )
    
    return logging.getLogger(__name__)
```

## Examples

### ì™„ì „í•œ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì˜ˆì‹œ

```python
# tests/test_api_e2e.py
import pytest
from pathlib import Path
import httpx
import json

@pytest.mark.e2e
def test_full_pipeline_e2e(client: httpx.Client):
    """
    ì „ì²´ íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    íŒŒì¼ ì—…ë¡œë“œ â†’ íŒŒì‹± â†’ Timeline ìƒì„± â†’ Issues ìƒì„± â†’ Export
    """
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    
    # 1. íŒŒì¼ ì—…ë¡œë“œ ë° íŒŒì‹±
    with open(input_file, "rb") as f:
        files = {"file": ("cursor_phase_6_3.md", f, "text/markdown")}
        parse_response = client.post("/api/parse", files=files)
    
    assert parse_response.status_code == 200
    parse_data = parse_response.json()
    
    # 2. Timeline ìƒì„±
    timeline_response = client.post(
        "/api/timeline",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"],
            "events": parse_data["events"],
            "session_meta": parse_data["session_meta"]
        }
    )
    assert timeline_response.status_code == 200
    timeline_data = timeline_response.json()
    
    # 3. Issues ìƒì„±
    issues_response = client.post(
        "/api/issues",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"],
            "events": parse_data["events"],
            "turns": parse_data["turns"]
        }
    )
    assert issues_response.status_code == 200
    issues_data = issues_response.json()
    
    # 4. Export í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    export_response = client.post(
        "/api/export/all",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"]
        }
    )
    assert export_response.status_code == 200
    
    # 5. ê²°ê³¼ ê²€ì¦
    assert len(timeline_data["timeline"]) > 0
    assert len(issues_data["issues"]) >= 0  # ì´ìŠˆê°€ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìŒ
    
    # 6. ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ìƒì„±
    report = {
        "test": "full_pipeline_e2e",
        "timeline_events": len(timeline_data["timeline"]),
        "issues": len(issues_data["issues"]),
        "status": "PASS"
    }
    
    print(json.dumps(report, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
```

## Checklist

### E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‘ì„± ì‹œ
- [ ] ì‹¤ì œ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ fixture ì‚¬ìš© (`test_server`)
- [ ] `httpx.Client` ì‚¬ìš© (TestClient ê¸ˆì§€)
- [ ] ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš© (Mock ê¸ˆì§€)
- [ ] ì •í•©ì„± ê²€ì¦ êµ¬í˜„
- [ ] íƒ€ë‹¹ì„± ê²€ì¦ êµ¬í˜„
- [ ] ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„ ë° ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ìƒì„±
- [ ] ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ í›„
- [ ] ìë™ìœ¼ë¡œ ìƒì„¸ ë³´ê³  ì¶œë ¥
- [ ] ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥
- [ ] ë¬¸ì œ ë°œê²¬ ì‹œ ì›ì¸ ë¶„ì„ í¬í•¨
- [ ] ì •ëŸ‰ì  ë°ì´í„° ì œì‹œ

# Testing Strategy

## Overview
í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸ëŠ” E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì¤‘ì‹¬ì˜ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì „ëµì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤. Phaseë³„ë¡œ ì ì ˆí•œ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë°©ì‹ì„ ì„ íƒí•˜ì—¬ í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ í”Œë¡œìš°ì™€ ë™ì¼í•˜ê²Œ ê²€ì¦í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

## Domain Knowledge

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì›ì¹™
1. **E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ìš°ì„ **: ëª¨ë“  í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš© í•„ìˆ˜
2. **ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©**: Mock ì‚¬ìš© ì ˆëŒ€ ê¸ˆì§€
3. **í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ í”Œë¡œìš° ë™ì¼**: ë°°í¬ í›„ ë¬¸ì œê°€ ì—†ìŒì„ ë³´ì¥
4. **ìë™ ë³´ê³  í•„ìˆ˜**: í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ í›„ ìƒì„¸ ë¶„ì„ ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸
5. **ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥ í•„ìˆ˜**: ëª¨ë“  E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥ (ë””ë²„ê¹… í•„ìˆ˜)
6. **ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼ ì €ì¥ í•„ìˆ˜**: íŒŒì‹±/ì¶”ì¶œ ê²°ê³¼ë¥¼ ìƒì„¸íˆ ì €ì¥ (ì‚¬ìš©ì ë¦¬ë·°/í”¼ë“œë°± í•„ìˆ˜)

### Phaseë³„ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ êµ¬ë¶„
- **Phase 2-5**: ëª¨ë“ˆ ì§ì ‘ í˜¸ì¶œ (ì„œë²„ ë¶ˆí•„ìš”)
  - íŒŒì„œ, ì´ë²¤íŠ¸ ì •ê·œí™”, Timeline/Issues ë¹Œë” ë“±ì€ ëª¨ë“ˆ ì§ì ‘ í˜¸ì¶œ
  - ì„œë²„ ì‹œì‘ ì˜¤ë²„í—¤ë“œ ì—†ì´ ë¹ ë¥¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ê°€ëŠ¥
- **Phase 6+**: ì‹¤ì œ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ (API í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ í•„ìˆ˜)
  - API ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ì‹¤ì œ uvicorn ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ í•„ìˆ˜
  - HTTP ë ˆë²¨ í†µí•© ê²€ì¦ í•„ìš”

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°
- ì‹¤ì œ Cursor export íŒŒì¼: `docs/cursor_phase_6_3.md`
- ê° Phaseë³„ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ì—ì„œ ë™ì¼ íŒŒì¼ ì‚¬ìš©

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë‹¨ê³„ë³„ ê²€ì¦
- **ì •í•©ì„± ê²€ì¦**: êµ¬ì¡°ì  ì •í™•ì„± í™•ì¸
- **íƒ€ë‹¹ì„± ê²€ì¦**: ì‹¤ì œ ìƒí™©ì—ì„œì˜ í’ˆì§ˆ í™•ì¸
- **ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„**: ìƒì„¸ ë¶„ì„ ë° ê°œì„ ì  ë„ì¶œ

## Standards & Conventions

### 1. íŒŒì¼ êµ¬ì¡°
```

â”œâ”€â”€ fixtures/
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ cursor_phase_6_3.md    # ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°
â”œâ”€â”€ golden/
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ parser_expected.json
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ timeline_expected.json
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ issues_expected.json
â”œâ”€â”€ logs/                        # ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ (ìë™ ìƒì„±)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ test_parser_e2e_20250101_120000.log
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ ...
â”œâ”€â”€ results/                     # ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼ (ìë™ ìƒì„±)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ parser_e2e_20250101_120000.json
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ ...
â”œâ”€â”€ reports/                     # ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ (ìë™ ìƒì„±)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ parser_e2e_report.json
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ ...
â”œâ”€â”€ conftest_e2e.py             # E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ fixture
â”œâ”€â”€ test_parser_e2e.py

â”œâ”€â”€ test_timeline_issues_e2e.py

â””â”€â”€ test_api_e2e.py
```

### 2. E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ Fixture

```python
# tests/conftest_e2e.py
import pytest
import subprocess
import time
import httpx
from pathlib import Path

@pytest.fixture(scope="session")
def test_server():
    """
    ì‹¤ì œ uvicorn ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ fixture
    """
    # ì„œë²„ ì‹œì‘
    process = subprocess.Popen(
        ["poetry", "run", "uvicorn", "backend.main:app", "--host", "0.0.0.0", "--port", "8000"],
        cwd=Path(__file__).parent.parent,
        stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
        stderr=subprocess.PIPE
    )
    
    # ì„œë²„ ì¤€ë¹„ ëŒ€ê¸°
    max_retries = 30
    for _ in range(max_retries):
        try:
            response = httpx.get("http://localhost:8000/health", timeout=1.0)
            if response.status_code == 200:
                break
        except:
            time.sleep(0.5)
    else:
        process.terminate()
        raise RuntimeError("Server failed to start")
    
    yield process
    
    # ì„œë²„ ì¢…ë£Œ
    process.terminate()
    process.wait()

@pytest.fixture
def client(test_server):
    """
    httpx.Client fixture (ì‹¤ì œ HTTP ìš”ì²­)
    """
    return httpx.Client(base_url="http://localhost:8000", timeout=30.0)
```

### 3. E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ íŒ¨í„´

```python
# tests/test_parser_e2e.py
import pytest
from pathlib import Path
from backend.parser import parse_markdown

def test_parser_e2e():
    """
    ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°ë¡œ ì „ì²´ íŒŒì„œ íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # 1. ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„° ë¡œë“œ
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    text = input_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8')
    
    # 2. íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤í–‰
    result = parse_markdown(text, source_doc=str(input_file))
    
    # 3. ì •í•©ì„± ê²€ì¦
    assert result["session_meta"] is not None
    assert result["session_meta"].session_id is not None
    assert len(result["turns"]) > 0
    
    # Session Meta ì¶”ì¶œ ì •í™•ì„±
    assert result["session_meta"].phase is not None or result["session_meta"].phase is None
    # (phaseê°€ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìœ¼ë¯€ë¡œ Noneë„ í—ˆìš©)
    
    # Turn ë¸”ë¡ ë¶„í•  ì •í™•ì„±
    user_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "User"]
    cursor_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "Cursor"]
    unknown_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "Unknown"]
    
    assert len(user_turns) > 0, "User turns should exist"
    assert len(cursor_turns) > 0, "Cursor turns should exist"
    
    # Unknown ë¹„ìœ¨ ê²€ì¦
    unknown_ratio = len(unknown_turns) / len(result["turns"])
    assert unknown_ratio < 0.2, f"Unknown speaker ratio too high: {unknown_ratio:.1%}"
    
    # ì½”ë“œ ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ ì •í™•ì„±
    all_code_blocks = []
    for turn in result["turns"]:
        all_code_blocks.extend(turn.code_blocks)
    
    assert len(all_code_blocks) > 0, "Code blocks should be extracted"
    
    # 4. íƒ€ë‹¹ì„± ê²€ì¦
    # íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤íŒ¨ìœ¨ ê²€ì¦
    assert unknown_ratio < 0.2, "Parse failure rate too high"
    
    # 5. ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„ ë° í”¼ë“œë°±
    print(f"\n[Parser E2E Test Results]")
    print(f"Total turns: {len(result['turns'])}")
    print(f"User turns: {len(user_turns)}")
    print(f"Cursor turns: {len(cursor_turns)}")
    print(f"Unknown turns: {len(unknown_turns)} ({unknown_ratio:.1%})")
    print(f"Code blocks: {len(all_code_blocks)}")
    print(f"Artifacts: {len(result.get('artifacts', []))}")
```

### 4. API E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ íŒ¨í„´

```python
# tests/test_api_e2e.py
import pytest
from pathlib import Path
import httpx

def test_parse_endpoint_e2e(client: httpx.Client):
    """
    POST /api/parse ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ íŒŒì¼
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    
    with open(input_file, "rb") as f:
        files = {"file": ("cursor_phase_6_3.md", f, "text/markdown")}
        response = client.post("/api/parse", files=files)
    
    assert response.status_code == 200
    
    data = response.json()
    
    # ì‘ë‹µ ìŠ¤í‚¤ë§ˆ ê²€ì¦
    assert "session_meta" in data
    assert "turns" in data
    assert "events" in data
    
    # íŒŒì‹± ê²°ê³¼ ì •í™•ì„±
    assert data["session_meta"]["session_id"] is not None
    assert len(data["turns"]) > 0

def test_timeline_endpoint_e2e(client: httpx.Client):
    """
    POST /api/timeline ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # 1. ë¨¼ì € íŒŒì‹±
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    
    with open(input_file, "rb") as f:
        files = {"file": ("cursor_phase_6_3.md", f, "text/markdown")}
        parse_response = client.post("/api/parse", files=files)
    
    parse_data = parse_response.json()
    
    # 2. Timeline ìƒì„±
    timeline_response = client.post(
        "/api/timeline",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"],
            "events": parse_data["events"],
            "session_meta": parse_data["session_meta"]
        }
    )
    
    assert timeline_response.status_code == 200
    
    timeline_data = timeline_response.json()
    
    # Timeline JSON êµ¬ì¡° ê²€ì¦
    assert "session_meta" in timeline_data
    assert "timeline" in timeline_data
    assert len(timeline_data["timeline"]) > 0
    
    # Artifact/Snippet ì—°ê²° í™•ì¸
    for event in timeline_data["timeline"]:
        assert "seq" in event
        assert "type" in event
        assert "summary" in event
```

### 5. í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ í›„ ìë™ ë³´ê³ 

```python
# tests/test_parser_e2e.py
def test_parser_e2e_with_report():
    """
    í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ í›„ ìƒì„¸ ë³´ê³  í¬í•¨
    """
    # ... í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ ...
    
    # ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„
    report = {
        "test_name": "parser_e2e",
        "input_file": str(input_file),
        "results": {
            "total_turns": len(result["turns"]),
            "user_turns": len(user_turns),
            "cursor_turns": len(cursor_turns),
            "unknown_ratio": unknown_ratio,
            "code_blocks": len(all_code_blocks),
            "artifacts": len(result.get("artifacts", []))
        },
        "warnings": [],
        "errors": []
    }
    
    if unknown_ratio > 0.2:
        report["warnings"].append(
            f"High Unknown speaker ratio: {unknown_ratio:.1%}"
        )
    
    # ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ì¶œë ¥
    import json
    print("\n" + "="*50)
    print("E2E Test Report")
    print("="*50)
    print(json.dumps(report, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
    print("="*50)
    
    # ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥
    report_file = Path(__file__).parent / "reports" / "parser_e2e_report.json"
    report_file.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    report_file.write_text(
        json.dumps(report, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False),
        encoding='utf-8'
    )
```

## Implementation Patterns

### Pattern 1: Golden íŒŒì¼ ë¹„êµ

```python
# tests/test_parser_e2e.py
def test_parser_golden_comparison():
    """
    Golden íŒŒì¼ê³¼ ë¹„êµí•˜ì—¬ íšŒê·€ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # ì‹¤ì œ íŒŒì‹±
    result = parse_markdown(text, source_doc)
    
    # Golden íŒŒì¼ ë¡œë“œ
    golden_file = Path(__file__).parent / "golden" / "parser_expected.json"
    if golden_file.exists():
        expected = json.loads(golden_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
        
        # ë¹„êµ (ì£¼ìš” í•„ë“œë§Œ)
        assert result["session_meta"].session_id == expected["session_meta"]["session_id"]
        assert len(result["turns"]) == len(expected["turns"])
    else:
        # Golden íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„± (ìµœì´ˆ 1íšŒ)
        golden_file.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        golden_file.write_text(
            json.dumps({
                "session_meta": result["session_meta"].dict(),
                "turns_count": len(result["turns"])
            }, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False),
            encoding='utf-8'
        )
```

### Pattern 2: ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥

```python
# í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ ì‹œ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ë¡œ ì €ì¥
import logging
from pathlib import Path

def setup_test_logging():
    """
    í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ìš© ë¡œê¹… ì„¤ì •
    """
    log_dir = Path(__file__).parent / "logs"
    log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    
    log_file = log_dir / f"test_{time.strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.log"
    
    logging.basicConfig(
        level=logging.DEBUG,
        format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
        handlers=[
            logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding='utf-8'),
            logging.StreamHandler()
        ]
    )
    
    return logging.getLogger(__name__)
```

## Examples

### ì™„ì „í•œ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì˜ˆì‹œ

```python
# tests/test_api_e2e.py
import pytest
from pathlib import Path
import httpx
import json

@pytest.mark.e2e
def test_full_pipeline_e2e(client: httpx.Client):
    """
    ì „ì²´ íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    íŒŒì¼ ì—…ë¡œë“œ â†’ íŒŒì‹± â†’ Timeline ìƒì„± â†’ Issues ìƒì„± â†’ Export
    """
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    
    # 1. íŒŒì¼ ì—…ë¡œë“œ ë° íŒŒì‹±
    with open(input_file, "rb") as f:
        files = {"file": ("cursor_phase_6_3.md", f, "text/markdown")}
        parse_response = client.post("/api/parse", files=files)
    
    assert parse_response.status_code == 200
    parse_data = parse_response.json()
    
    # 2. Timeline ìƒì„±
    timeline_response = client.post(
        "/api/timeline",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"],
            "events": parse_data["events"],
            "session_meta": parse_data["session_meta"]
        }
    )
    assert timeline_response.status_code == 200
    timeline_data = timeline_response.json()
    
    # 3. Issues ìƒì„±
    issues_response = client.post(
        "/api/issues",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"],
            "events": parse_data["events"],
            "turns": parse_data["turns"]
        }
    )
    assert issues_response.status_code == 200
    issues_data = issues_response.json()
    
    # 4. Export í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    export_response = client.post(
        "/api/export/all",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"]
        }
    )
    assert export_response.status_code == 200
    
    # 5. ê²°ê³¼ ê²€ì¦
    assert len(timeline_data["timeline"]) > 0
    assert len(issues_data["issues"]) >= 0  # ì´ìŠˆê°€ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìŒ
    
    # 6. ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ìƒì„±
    report = {
        "test": "full_pipeline_e2e",
        "timeline_events": len(timeline_data["timeline"]),
        "issues": len(issues_data["issues"]),
        "status": "PASS"
    }
    
    print(json.dumps(report, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
```

- [ ] íƒ€ë‹¹ì„± ê²€ì¦ êµ¬í˜„
- [ ] ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„ ë° ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ìƒì„±
- [ ] ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ í›„
- [ ] ìë™ìœ¼ë¡œ ìƒì„¸ ë³´ê³  ì¶œë ¥
- [ ] ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥
- [ ] ë¬¸ì œ ë°œê²¬ ì‹œ ì›ì¸ ë¶„ì„ í¬í•¨

# Testing Strategy

## Overview
í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸ëŠ” E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì¤‘ì‹¬ì˜ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì „ëµì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤. Phaseë³„ë¡œ ì ì ˆí•œ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë°©ì‹ì„ ì„ íƒí•˜ì—¬ í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ í”Œë¡œìš°ì™€ ë™ì¼í•˜ê²Œ ê²€ì¦í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

## Domain Knowledge

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì›ì¹™
1. **E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ìš°ì„ **: ëª¨ë“  í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš© í•„ìˆ˜
2. **ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©**: Mock ì‚¬ìš© ì ˆëŒ€ ê¸ˆì§€
3. **í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ í”Œë¡œìš° ë™ì¼**: ë°°í¬ í›„ ë¬¸ì œê°€ ì—†ìŒì„ ë³´ì¥
4. **ìë™ ë³´ê³  í•„ìˆ˜**: í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ í›„ ìƒì„¸ ë¶„ì„ ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸
5. **ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥ í•„ìˆ˜**: ëª¨ë“  E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥ (ë””ë²„ê¹… í•„ìˆ˜)
6. **ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼ ì €ì¥ í•„ìˆ˜**: íŒŒì‹±/ì¶”ì¶œ ê²°ê³¼ë¥¼ ìƒì„¸íˆ ì €ì¥ (ì‚¬ìš©ì ë¦¬ë·°/í”¼ë“œë°± í•„ìˆ˜)

### Phaseë³„ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ êµ¬ë¶„
- **Phase 2-5**: ëª¨ë“ˆ ì§ì ‘ í˜¸ì¶œ (ì„œë²„ ë¶ˆí•„ìš”)
  - íŒŒì„œ, ì´ë²¤íŠ¸ ì •ê·œí™”, Timeline/Issues ë¹Œë” ë“±ì€ ëª¨ë“ˆ ì§ì ‘ í˜¸ì¶œ
  - ì„œë²„ ì‹œì‘ ì˜¤ë²„í—¤ë“œ ì—†ì´ ë¹ ë¥¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ê°€ëŠ¥
- **Phase 6+**: ì‹¤ì œ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ (API í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ í•„ìˆ˜)
  - API ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ì‹¤ì œ uvicorn ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ í•„ìˆ˜
  - HTTP ë ˆë²¨ í†µí•© ê²€ì¦ í•„ìš”

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°
- ì‹¤ì œ Cursor export íŒŒì¼: `docs/cursor_phase_6_3.md`
- ê° Phaseë³„ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ì—ì„œ ë™ì¼ íŒŒì¼ ì‚¬ìš©

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë‹¨ê³„ë³„ ê²€ì¦
- **ì •í•©ì„± ê²€ì¦**: êµ¬ì¡°ì  ì •í™•ì„± í™•ì¸
- **íƒ€ë‹¹ì„± ê²€ì¦**: ì‹¤ì œ ìƒí™©ì—ì„œì˜ í’ˆì§ˆ í™•ì¸
- **ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„**: ìƒì„¸ ë¶„ì„ ë° ê°œì„ ì  ë„ì¶œ

## Standards & Conventions

### 1. íŒŒì¼ êµ¬ì¡°
```
tests/
â”œâ”€â”€ fixtures/
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ cursor_phase_6_3.md    # ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°
â”œâ”€â”€ golden/
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ parser_expected.json
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ timeline_expected.json
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ issues_expected.json
â”œâ”€â”€ logs/                        # ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ (ìë™ ìƒì„±)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ test_parser_e2e_20250101_120000.log
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ ...
â”œâ”€â”€ results/                     # ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼ (ìë™ ìƒì„±)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ parser_e2e_20250101_120000.json
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ ...
â”œâ”€â”€ reports/                     # ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ (ìë™ ìƒì„±)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ parser_e2e_report.json
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ ...
â”œâ”€â”€ conftest_e2e.py             # E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ fixture
â”œâ”€â”€ test_parser_e2e.py
â”œâ”€â”€ test_event_normalizer_e2e.py
â”œâ”€â”€ test_timeline_issues_e2e.py
â”œâ”€â”€ test_snippet_e2e.py
â””â”€â”€ test_api_e2e.py
```

### 2. E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ Fixture

```python
# tests/conftest_e2e.py
import pytest
import subprocess
import time
import httpx
import logging
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime

# Phase 6+ ì „ìš©: ì‹¤ì œ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ fixture
@pytest.fixture(scope="session")
def test_server():
    """
    ì‹¤ì œ uvicorn ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ fixture (Phase 6+ API í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ìš©)
    """
    # ì„œë²„ ì‹œì‘
    process = subprocess.Popen(
        ["poetry", "run", "uvicorn", "backend.main:app", "--host", "0.0.0.0", "--port", "8000"],
        cwd=Path(__file__).parent.parent,
        stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
        stderr=subprocess.PIPE
    )
    
    # ì„œë²„ ì¤€ë¹„ ëŒ€ê¸°
    max_retries = 30
    for _ in range(max_retries):
        try:
            response = httpx.get("http://localhost:8000/health", timeout=1.0)
            if response.status_code == 200:
                break
        except:
            time.sleep(0.5)
    else:
        process.terminate()
        raise RuntimeError("Server failed to start")
    
    yield process
    
    # ì„œë²„ ì¢…ë£Œ
    process.terminate()
    process.wait()

@pytest.fixture
def client(test_server):
    """
    httpx.Client fixture (ì‹¤ì œ HTTP ìš”ì²­, Phase 6+ ì „ìš©)
    """
    return httpx.Client(base_url="http://localhost:8000", timeout=30.0)

# ëª¨ë“  E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ì— ìë™ ì ìš©: ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥
@pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
def setup_test_logging(request):
    """
    ëª¨ë“  E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ì— ìë™ìœ¼ë¡œ ë¡œê¹… ì„¤ì • (í•„ìˆ˜)
    """
    log_dir = Path(__file__).parent / "logs"
    log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
    test_name = request.node.name
    log_file = log_dir / f"{test_name}_{timestamp}.log"
    
    # ê¸°ì¡´ í•¸ë“¤ëŸ¬ ì œê±° (ì¤‘ë³µ ë°©ì§€)
    for handler in logging.root.handlers[:]:
        logging.root.removeHandler(handler)
    
    logging.basicConfig(
        level=logging.DEBUG,
        format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
        handlers=[
            logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding='utf-8'),
            logging.StreamHandler()
        ],
        force=True
    )
    
    logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    logger.info(f"Test started: {test_name}")
    logger.info(f"Log file: {log_file}")
    
    yield
    
    # í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì¢…ë£Œ í›„ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ê²½ë¡œ ì¶œë ¥
    logger.info(f"Test completed: {test_name}")
    print(f"\n[LOG] Test log saved to: {log_file}")
```

### 3. E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ íŒ¨í„´

```python
# tests/test_parser_e2e.py
import pytest
from pathlib import Path
from backend.parser import parse_markdown

def test_parser_e2e():
    """
    ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°ë¡œ ì „ì²´ íŒŒì„œ íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # 1. ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„° ë¡œë“œ
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    text = input_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8')
    
    # 2. íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤í–‰
    result = parse_markdown(text, source_doc=str(input_file))
    
    # 3. ì •í•©ì„± ê²€ì¦
    assert result["session_meta"] is not None
    assert result["session_meta"].session_id is not None
    assert len(result["turns"]) > 0
    
    # Session Meta ì¶”ì¶œ ì •í™•ì„±
    assert result["session_meta"].phase is not None or result["session_meta"].phase is None
    # (phaseê°€ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìœ¼ë¯€ë¡œ Noneë„ í—ˆìš©)
    
    # Turn ë¸”ë¡ ë¶„í•  ì •í™•ì„±
    user_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "User"]
    cursor_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "Cursor"]
    unknown_turns = [t for t in result["turns"] if t.speaker == "Unknown"]
    
    assert len(user_turns) > 0, "User turns should exist"
    assert len(cursor_turns) > 0, "Cursor turns should exist"
    
    # Unknown ë¹„ìœ¨ ê²€ì¦
    unknown_ratio = len(unknown_turns) / len(result["turns"])
    assert unknown_ratio < 0.2, f"Unknown speaker ratio too high: {unknown_ratio:.1%}"
    
    # ì½”ë“œ ìŠ¤ë‹ˆí« ì¶”ì¶œ ì •í™•ì„±
    all_code_blocks = []
    for turn in result["turns"]:
        all_code_blocks.extend(turn.code_blocks)
    
    assert len(all_code_blocks) > 0, "Code blocks should be extracted"
    
    # 4. íƒ€ë‹¹ì„± ê²€ì¦
    # íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤íŒ¨ìœ¨ ê²€ì¦
    assert unknown_ratio < 0.2, "Parse failure rate too high"
    
    # 5. ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„ ë° í”¼ë“œë°±
    print(f"\n[Parser E2E Test Results]")
    print(f"Total turns: {len(result['turns'])}")
    print(f"User turns: {len(user_turns)}")
    print(f"Cursor turns: {len(cursor_turns)}")
    print(f"Unknown turns: {len(unknown_turns)} ({unknown_ratio:.1%})")
    print(f"Code blocks: {len(all_code_blocks)}")
    print(f"Artifacts: {len(result.get('artifacts', []))}")
```

### 4. API E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ íŒ¨í„´

```python
# tests/test_api_e2e.py
import pytest
from pathlib import Path
import httpx

def test_parse_endpoint_e2e(client: httpx.Client):
    """
    POST /api/parse ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ íŒŒì¼
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    
    with open(input_file, "rb") as f:
        files = {"file": ("cursor_phase_6_3.md", f, "text/markdown")}
        response = client.post("/api/parse", files=files)
    
    assert response.status_code == 200
    
    data = response.json()
    
    # ì‘ë‹µ ìŠ¤í‚¤ë§ˆ ê²€ì¦
    assert "session_meta" in data
    assert "turns" in data
    assert "events" in data
    
    # íŒŒì‹± ê²°ê³¼ ì •í™•ì„±
    assert data["session_meta"]["session_id"] is not None
    assert len(data["turns"]) > 0

def test_timeline_endpoint_e2e(client: httpx.Client):
    """
    POST /api/timeline ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # 1. ë¨¼ì € íŒŒì‹±
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    
    with open(input_file, "rb") as f:
        files = {"file": ("cursor_phase_6_3.md", f, "text/markdown")}
        parse_response = client.post("/api/parse", files=files)
    
    parse_data = parse_response.json()
    
    # 2. Timeline ìƒì„±
    timeline_response = client.post(
        "/api/timeline",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"],
            "events": parse_data["events"],
            "session_meta": parse_data["session_meta"]
        }
    )
    
    assert timeline_response.status_code == 200
    
    timeline_data = timeline_response.json()
    
    # Timeline JSON êµ¬ì¡° ê²€ì¦
    assert "session_meta" in timeline_data
    assert "timeline" in timeline_data
    assert len(timeline_data["timeline"]) > 0
    
    # Artifact/Snippet ì—°ê²° í™•ì¸
    for event in timeline_data["timeline"]:
        assert "seq" in event
        assert "type" in event
        assert "summary" in event
```

### 5. í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ í›„ ìë™ ë³´ê³ 

```python
# tests/test_parser_e2e.py
def test_parser_e2e_with_report():
    """
    í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ í›„ ìƒì„¸ ë³´ê³  í¬í•¨
    """
    # ... í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ ...
    
    # ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„
    report = {
        "test_name": "parser_e2e",
        "input_file": str(input_file),
        "results": {
            "total_turns": len(result["turns"]),
            "user_turns": len(user_turns),
            "cursor_turns": len(cursor_turns),
            "unknown_ratio": unknown_ratio,
            "code_blocks": len(all_code_blocks),
            "artifacts": len(result.get("artifacts", []))
        },
        "warnings": [],
        "errors": []
    }
    
    if unknown_ratio > 0.2:
        report["warnings"].append(
            f"High Unknown speaker ratio: {unknown_ratio:.1%}"
        )
    
    # ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ì¶œë ¥
    import json
    print("\n" + "="*50)
    print("E2E Test Report")
    print("="*50)
    print(json.dumps(report, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
    print("="*50)
    
    # ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥
    report_file = Path(__file__).parent / "reports" / "parser_e2e_report.json"
    report_file.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    report_file.write_text(
        json.dumps(report, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False),
        encoding='utf-8'
    )
```

## Implementation Patterns

### Pattern 1: Golden íŒŒì¼ ë¹„êµ

```python
# tests/test_parser_e2e.py
def test_parser_golden_comparison():
    """
    Golden íŒŒì¼ê³¼ ë¹„êµí•˜ì—¬ íšŒê·€ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    """
    # ì‹¤ì œ íŒŒì‹±
    result = parse_markdown(text, source_doc)
    
    # Golden íŒŒì¼ ë¡œë“œ
    golden_file = Path(__file__).parent / "golden" / "parser_expected.json"
    if golden_file.exists():
        expected = json.loads(golden_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
        
        # ë¹„êµ (ì£¼ìš” í•„ë“œë§Œ)
        assert result["session_meta"].session_id == expected["session_meta"]["session_id"]
        assert len(result["turns"]) == len(expected["turns"])
    else:
        # Golden íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„± (ìµœì´ˆ 1íšŒ)
        golden_file.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        golden_file.write_text(
            json.dumps({
                "session_meta": result["session_meta"].dict(),
                "turns_count": len(result["turns"])
            }, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False),
            encoding='utf-8'
        )
```

### Pattern 2: ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥

```python
# í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ ì‹œ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ë¡œ ì €ì¥
import logging
from pathlib import Path

def setup_test_logging():
    """
    í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ìš© ë¡œê¹… ì„¤ì •
    """
    log_dir = Path(__file__).parent / "logs"
    log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    
    log_file = log_dir / f"test_{time.strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.log"
    
    logging.basicConfig(
        level=logging.DEBUG,
        format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
        handlers=[
            logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding='utf-8'),
            logging.StreamHandler()
        ]
    )
    
    return logging.getLogger(__name__)
```

## Examples

### ì™„ì „í•œ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì˜ˆì‹œ

```python
# tests/test_api_e2e.py
import pytest
from pathlib import Path
import httpx
import json

@pytest.mark.e2e
def test_full_pipeline_e2e(client: httpx.Client):
    """
    ì „ì²´ íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    íŒŒì¼ ì—…ë¡œë“œ â†’ íŒŒì‹± â†’ Timeline ìƒì„± â†’ Issues ìƒì„± â†’ Export
    """
    input_file = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "docs" / "cursor_phase_6_3.md"
    
    # 1. íŒŒì¼ ì—…ë¡œë“œ ë° íŒŒì‹±
    with open(input_file, "rb") as f:
        files = {"file": ("cursor_phase_6_3.md", f, "text/markdown")}
        parse_response = client.post("/api/parse", files=files)
    
    assert parse_response.status_code == 200
    parse_data = parse_response.json()
    
    # 2. Timeline ìƒì„±
    timeline_response = client.post(
        "/api/timeline",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"],
            "events": parse_data["events"],
            "session_meta": parse_data["session_meta"]
        }
    )
    assert timeline_response.status_code == 200
    timeline_data = timeline_response.json()
    
    # 3. Issues ìƒì„±
    issues_response = client.post(
        "/api/issues",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"],
            "events": parse_data["events"],
            "turns": parse_data["turns"]
        }
    )
    assert issues_response.status_code == 200
    issues_data = issues_response.json()
    
    # 4. Export í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    export_response = client.post(
        "/api/export/all",
        json={
            "session_id": parse_data["session_meta"]["session_id"]
        }
    )
    assert export_response.status_code == 200
    
    # 5. ê²°ê³¼ ê²€ì¦
    assert len(timeline_data["timeline"]) > 0
    assert len(issues_data["issues"]) >= 0  # ì´ìŠˆê°€ ì—†ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆìŒ
    
    # 6. ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ìƒì„±
    report = {
        "test": "full_pipeline_e2e",
        "timeline_events": len(timeline_data["timeline"]),
        "issues": len(issues_data["issues"]),
        "status": "PASS"
    }
    
    print(json.dumps(report, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
```

# Testing Strategy

## Overview
í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸ëŠ” E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì¤‘ì‹¬ì˜ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì „ëµì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤. Phaseë³„ë¡œ ì ì ˆí•œ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë°©ì‹ì„ ì„ íƒí•˜ì—¬ í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ í”Œë¡œìš°ì™€ ë™ì¼í•˜ê²Œ ê²€ì¦í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

## Domain Knowledge

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì›ì¹™
1. **E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ìš°ì„ **: ëª¨ë“  í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš© í•„ìˆ˜
2. **ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©**: Mock ì‚¬ìš© ì ˆëŒ€ ê¸ˆì§€
3. **í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ í”Œë¡œìš° ë™ì¼**: ë°°í¬ í›„ ë¬¸ì œê°€ ì—†ìŒì„ ë³´ì¥
4. **ìë™ ë³´ê³  í•„ìˆ˜**: í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ í›„ ìƒì„¸ ë¶„ì„ ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸
5. **ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥ í•„ìˆ˜**: ëª¨ë“  E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì €ì¥ (ë””ë²„ê¹… í•„ìˆ˜)
6. **ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼ ì €ì¥ í•„ìˆ˜**: íŒŒì‹±/ì¶”ì¶œ ê²°ê³¼ë¥¼ ìƒì„¸íˆ ì €ì¥ (ì‚¬ìš©ì ë¦¬ë·°/í”¼ë“œë°± í•„ìˆ˜)

### Phaseë³„ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ êµ¬ë¶„
- **Phase 2-5**: ëª¨ë“ˆ ì§ì ‘ í˜¸ì¶œ (ì„œë²„ ë¶ˆí•„ìš”)
  - íŒŒì„œ, ì´ë²¤íŠ¸ ì •ê·œí™”, Timeline/Issues ë¹Œë” ë“±ì€ ëª¨ë“ˆ ì§ì ‘ í˜¸ì¶œ
  - ì„œë²„ ì‹œì‘ ì˜¤ë²„í—¤ë“œ ì—†ì´ ë¹ ë¥¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ê°€ëŠ¥
- **Phase 6+**: ì‹¤ì œ ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ (API í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ í•„ìˆ˜)
  - API ì—”ë“œí¬ì¸íŠ¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ëŠ” ì‹¤ì œ uvicorn ì„œë²„ ì‹¤í–‰ í•„ìˆ˜
  - HTTP ë ˆë²¨ í†µí•© ê²€ì¦ í•„ìš”

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°
- ì‹¤ì œ Cursor export íŒŒì¼: `docs/cursor_phase_6_3.md`
- ê° Phaseë³„ E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ì—ì„œ ë™ì¼ íŒŒì¼ ì‚¬ìš©

### í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë‹¨ê³„ë³„ ê²€ì¦
- **ì •í•©ì„± ê²€ì¦**: êµ¬ì¡°ì  ì •í™•ì„± í™•ì¸

## Standards & Conventions

### 1. íŒŒì¼ êµ¬ì¡°
```
tests/
â”œâ”€â”€ fixtures/
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ cursor_phase_6_3.md    # ì‹¤ì œ ì…ë ¥ ë°ì´í„°
â”œâ”€â”€ golden/
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ parser_expected.json
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ timeline_expected.json
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ issues_expected.json
â”œâ”€â”€ logs/                        # ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ (ìë™ ìƒì„±)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ test_parser_e2e_20250101_120000.log
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ ...
â”œâ”€â”€ results/                     # ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼ (ìë™ ìƒì„±)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ parser_e2e_20250101_120000.json
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ ...
â”œâ”€â”€ reports/                     # ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ (ìë™ ìƒì„±)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ parser_e2e_report.json
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ ...
â”œâ”€â”€ conftest_e2e.py             # E2E í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ fixture
â”œâ”€â”€ test_parser_e2e.py
â”œâ”€â”€ test_event_normalizer_e2e.py
â”œâ”€â”€ test_timeline_issues_e2e.py
